./Controller.py:#!/usr/bin/env python3
./Controller.py:import kopf
./Controller.py:import requests
./Controller.py:import os
./Controller.py:GPU_OPTIMIZER_URL = os.environ.get("GPU_OPTIMIZER_URL", "http://localhost:10000")
./Controller.py:@kopf.on.create('energy.gpu-optimizer.io', 'v1', 'powercaps')
./Controller.py:def apply_power_cap(spec, **kwargs):
./Controller.py:    gpu_id = spec.get('gpu_id')
./Controller.py:    power_limit = spec.get('power_limit_watts')
./Controller.py:    workload = spec.get('workload_type', 'inference')
./Controller.py:    
./Controller.py:    resp = requests.post(
./Controller.py:        f"{GPU_OPTIMIZER_URL}/k8s/power-cap",
./Controller.py:        params={"gpu_id": gpu_id, "power_limit_watts": power_limit, "workload_type": workload}
./Controller.py:    )
./Controller.py:    
./Controller.py:    if resp.status_code == 200:
./Controller.py:        return {"message": f"Power cap {power_limit}W applied to GPU {gpu_id}"}
./Controller.py:    else:
./Controller.py:        raise kopf.PermanentError(f"Failed: {resp.text}")
./Controller.py:@kopf.on.delete('energy.gpu-optimizer.io', 'v1', 'powercaps')
./Controller.py:def remove_power_cap(spec, **kwargs):
./Controller.py:    gpu_id = spec.get('gpu_id')
./Controller.py:    # Reset power cap to default (250W)
./Controller.py:    requests.post(f"{GPU_OPTIMIZER_URL}/k8s/power-cap", params={"gpu_id": gpu_id, "power_limit_watts": 250})
./Controller.py:    return {"message": f"Power cap removed from GPU {gpu_id}"}

./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:    def send_to_backend_with_retry(self, metrics, max_retries=3):
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        """Send metrics with exponential backoff retry"""
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        headers = {
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            "Content-Type": "application/json"
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        }
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        for attempt in range(max_retries):
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            try:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                response = requests.post(
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    f"{self.backend_url}/api/v1/metrics",
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    json=metrics,
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    headers=headers,
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    timeout=10
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                )
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                if response.status_code == 200:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    self.consecutive_failures = 0
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    return True
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                elif response.status_code == 401:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    print(f"❌ Authentication failed: Invalid API key")
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    return False
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                else:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    print(f"⚠️ Backend returned {response.status_code}")
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                    
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            except requests.exceptions.Timeout:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                print(f"⚠️ Timeout (attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries})")
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            except requests.exceptions.ConnectionError:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                print(f"⚠️ Connection error (attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries})")
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            except Exception as e:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                print(f"⚠️ Error: {e} (attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries})")
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:            if attempt < max_retries - 1:
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                wait_time = 2 ** attempt
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:                time.sleep(wait_time)
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        self.consecutive_failures += 1
./ai-engine/gpu_monitor_agent.py:        return False

./ai-engine/main.py:# ========== ENGINE 1: TRUE EFFICIENCY ==========
./ai-engine/main.py:def calculate_true_efficiency(metrics_history: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(metrics_history) < 2:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": "Insufficient data", "samples": len(metrics_history)}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    util_series, power_series, timestamps = [], [], []
./ai-engine/main.py:    for m in metrics_history:
./ai-engine/main.py:        if m.get('gpus') and len(m['gpus']) > 0:
./ai-engine/main.py:            gpu = m['gpus'][0]
./ai-engine/main.py:            util_series.append(gpu.get('utilization_percent', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:            power_series.append(gpu.get('power_draw_watts', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:            timestamps.append(m.get('timestamp', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(util_series) < 2:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": "No valid GPU data"}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    total_time = timestamps[-1] - timestamps[0] if timestamps[-1] > timestamps[0] else len(util_series)
./ai-engine/main.py:    useful_compute_time = sum(1 for u in util_series if u > 5)
./ai-engine/main.py:    avg_util = np.mean(util_series) / 100.0
./ai-engine/main.py:    avg_power = max(np.mean(power_series), 1.0)
./ai-engine/main.py:    util_variance = np.var(util_series)
./ai-engine/main.py:    normalized_variance = min(util_variance / 100.0, 1.0)
./ai-engine/main.py:    consistency = 1.0 - normalized_variance
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    efficiency = (useful_compute_time / total_time) * (avg_util / avg_power) * consistency
./ai-engine/main.py:    efficiency = max(0.0, min(1.0, efficiency))
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    return {
./ai-engine/main.py:        "efficiency_score": round(efficiency, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "efficiency_percentage": round(efficiency * 100, 2),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "useful_compute_ratio": round(useful_compute_time / total_time, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "consistency": round(consistency, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "samples_analyzed": len(util_series)
./ai-engine/main.py:    }
./ai-engine/main.py:# ========== ENGINE 2: IDLE DETECTION ==========
./ai-engine/main.py:def calculate_idle_waste(metrics_history: List[Dict], cost_per_hour: float = 3.50) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(metrics_history) < 10:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": "Insufficient data", "samples": len(metrics_history)}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    util_series, power_series = [], []
./ai-engine/main.py:    for m in metrics_history:
./ai-engine/main.py:        if m.get('gpus') and len(m['gpus']) > 0:
./ai-engine/main.py:            gpu = m['gpus'][0]
./ai-engine/main.py:            util_series.append(gpu.get('utilization_percent', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:            power_series.append(gpu.get('power_draw_watts', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    idle_periods, current_start = [], None
./ai-engine/main.py:    for i, u in enumerate(util_series):
./ai-engine/main.py:        if u < 5 and current_start is None:
./ai-engine/main.py:            current_start = i
./ai-engine/main.py:        elif u >= 5 and current_start is not None:
./ai-engine/main.py:            duration = i - current_start
./ai-engine/main.py:            if duration >= 2:
./ai-engine/main.py:                idle_periods.append(duration)
./ai-engine/main.py:            current_start = None
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    total_idle = sum(idle_periods)
./ai-engine/main.py:    total_time = len(util_series)
./ai-engine/main.py:    idle_pct = (total_idle / total_time) * 100
./ai-engine/main.py:    cost_waste = total_idle * (cost_per_hour / 3600)
./ai-engine/main.py:    false_idle = sum(1 for u, p in zip(util_series, power_series) if u < 5 and p > 120)
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    if idle_pct > 30:
./ai-engine/main.py:        rec = f"GPU idle {idle_pct:.1f}% → reduce instances"

./ai-engine/main.py:    else:

./ai-engine/main.py:# ========== ENGINE 3: BURST DETECTION ==========
./ai-engine/main.py:def detect_compute_bursts(metrics_history: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(metrics_history) < 10:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": "Insufficient data", "burst_count": 0}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    power_series, util_series = [], []
./ai-engine/main.py:    for m in metrics_history:
./ai-engine/main.py:        if m.get('gpus') and len(m['gpus']) > 0:
./ai-engine/main.py:            gpu = m['gpus'][0]
./ai-engine/main.py:            power_series.append(gpu.get('power_draw_watts', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:            util_series.append(gpu.get('utilization_percent', 0))
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    bursts, confidence = [], {"HIGH": 0, "MEDIUM": 0, "LOW": 0}
./ai-engine/main.py:    for i in range(1, len(power_series)):
./ai-engine/main.py:        power_delta = power_series[i] - power_series[i-1]
./ai-engine/main.py:        util_delta = abs(util_series[i] - util_series[i-1])
./ai-engine/main.py:        
./ai-engine/main.py:        if power_delta > 50 and util_delta < 5:
./ai-engine/main.py:            if power_delta > 100:
./ai-engine/main.py:                conf = "HIGH"
./ai-engine/main.py:            elif power_delta > 50:
./ai-engine/main.py:                conf = "MEDIUM"
./ai-engine/main.py:            else:
./ai-engine/main.py:                conf = "LOW"
./ai-engine/main.py:            confidence[conf] += 1
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    minutes = len(metrics_history) / 60
./ai-engine/main.py:    bursts_per_min = len(bursts) / minutes if minutes > 0 else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    return {
./ai-engine/main.py:        "burst_count": len(bursts),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "bursts_per_minute": round(bursts_per_min, 2),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "peak_power_watts": round(max(power_series), 1) if power_series else 0,
./ai-engine/main.py:        "confidence": confidence
./ai-engine/main.py:    }
./ai-engine/main.py:# ========== ENGINE 4: SAMPLING GAP ==========
./ai-engine/main.py:def estimate_sampling_gap(metrics_history: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    burst = detect_compute_bursts(metrics_history)
./ai-engine/main.py:    burst_count = burst.get("burst_count", 0)
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    missed_sec = burst_count * 0.05
./ai-engine/main.py:    total_time = len(metrics_history)
./ai-engine/main.py:    gap_pct = (missed_sec / total_time) * 100 if total_time > 0 else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    if gap_pct > 5:
./ai-engine/main.py:        severity, msg = "HIGH", f"Monitoring misses ~{gap_pct:.1f}% of compute activity"
./ai-engine/main.py:    elif gap_pct > 1:
./ai-engine/main.py:        severity, msg = "MEDIUM", f"Monitoring misses ~{gap_pct:.1f}% of compute activity"
./ai-engine/main.py:    else:
./ai-engine/main.py:        severity, msg = "LOW", f"Sampling gap is {gap_pct:.2f}% - acceptable"
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    return {
./ai-engine/main.py:        "sampling_gap_percent": round(gap_pct, 2),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "severity": severity,
./ai-engine/main.py:        "message": msg,
./ai-engine/main.py:        "estimated_missed_seconds": round(missed_sec, 3),

./ai-engine/main.py:def evaluate_alerts(metrics_history: List[Dict], cooldown: int = 300) -> Dict:

./ai-engine/main.py:        if key not in _last_alert or (now - _last_alert[key]) > cooldown:
./ai-engine/main.py:            alerts.append({"type": "TEMPERATURE", "severity": "CRITICAL", "value": temp, "message": f"GPU at {temp}°C - immediate action"})
./ai-engine/main.py:            _last_alert[key] = now
./ai-engine/main.py:    elif temp > 75:
./ai-engine/main.py:        key = f"{cluster}_temp_warn"
./ai-engine/main.py:        if key not in _last_alert or (now - _last_alert[key]) > cooldown:
./ai-engine/main.py:            alerts.append({"type": "TEMPERATURE", "severity": "WARNING", "value": temp, "message": f"GPU at {temp}°C - reduce workload"})
./ai-engine/main.py:            _last_alert[key] = now
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    if util < 10:
./ai-engine/main.py:        key = f"{cluster}_idle"
./ai-engine/main.py:        if key not in _last_alert or (now - _last_alert[key]) > cooldown:
./ai-engine/main.py:            alerts.append({"type": "IDLE", "severity": "INFO", "value": util, "message": f"GPU at {util}% utilization - potential waste"})
./ai-engine/main.py:            _last_alert[key] = now
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    return {"alert_count": len(alerts), "alerts": alerts}

./ai-engine/main.py:def detect_power_state(metrics_history: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(metrics_history) < 10:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": "Insufficient data"}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    low_util_high_power = 0

./ai-engine/main.py:        if m.get('gpus') and len(m['gpus']) > 0:
./ai-engine/main.py:            gpu = m['gpus'][0]

./ai-engine/main.py:    if low_util_high_power > 30:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"power_state": "HIGH_RESIDENCY_STATE", "severity": "INFO", "message": "GPU in high-power residency state (normal datacenter behavior)", "samples": low_util_high_power}
./ai-engine/main.py:    elif low_util_high_power > 10:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"power_state": "INTERMITTENT_HIGH_POWER", "severity": "LOW", "message": "GPU shows intermittent high power at low utilization", "samples": low_util_high_power}
./ai-engine/main.py:    else:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"power_state": "NORMAL", "severity": "OK", "message": "GPU power state normal", "samples": low_util_high_power}
./ai-engine/main.py:# ========== ENGINE 8: DELTA TRACKER ==========
./ai-engine/main.py:def calculate_efficiency_delta(metrics_history: List[Dict], baseline_sec: int = 60, after_sec: int = 60) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/main.py:    if len(metrics_history) < baseline_sec + after_sec:
./ai-engine/main.py:        return {"error": f"Insufficient data. Need {baseline_sec + after_sec} samples, have {len(metrics_history)}"}
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    baseline, after = metrics_history[:baseline_sec], metrics_history[-after_sec:]
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    def avg_util(data): utils = [m['gpus'][0].get('utilization_percent', 0) for m in data if m.get('gpus')]; return sum(utils)/len(utils) if utils else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    def avg_power(data): powers = [m['gpus'][0].get('power_draw_watts', 0) for m in data if m.get('gpus')]; return sum(powers)/len(powers) if powers else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    base_util, after_util = avg_util(baseline), avg_util(after)
./ai-engine/main.py:    base_power, after_power = avg_power(baseline), avg_power(after)
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    base_eff = base_util / base_power if base_power > 0 else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    after_eff = after_util / after_power if after_power > 0 else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    delta = after_eff - base_eff
./ai-engine/main.py:    gain = (delta / base_eff) * 100 if base_eff > 0 else 0
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    if delta > 0: conclusion = "Workload scaling improved efficiency"
./ai-engine/main.py:    elif delta < 0: conclusion = "Workload scaling is inefficient - wasting power"
./ai-engine/main.py:    else: conclusion = "No change in efficiency"
./ai-engine/main.py:    
./ai-engine/main.py:    return {
./ai-engine/main.py:        "efficiency_delta": round(delta, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "efficiency_gain_percent": round(gain, 2),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "baseline_efficiency": round(base_eff, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "after_efficiency": round(after_eff, 4),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "baseline_util_pct": round(base_util, 1),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "after_util_pct": round(after_util, 1),
./ai-engine/main.py:        "conclusion": conclusion
./ai-engine/main.py:    }

./ai-engine/main.py:                await connection.send_json(message)
./ai-engine/main.py:            except:
./ai-engine/main.py:                self.disconnect(connection)

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:    def analyze(self, clusters: List[GPUState], grid_carbon_intensity: float = 0.45) -> List[Recommendation]:
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:        """
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:        Main optimization loop. Analyzes state → generates recommendations.
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:        """
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:        recommendations = []

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            # Store in history
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            self.history.append(cluster)
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            if len(self.history) > self.max_history:
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                self.history.pop(0)
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            # 1. THERMAL OPTIMIZATION
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            if cluster.temperature > 85:
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                recommendations.append(Recommendation(
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    id=f"thermal_crit_{cluster.id}",
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    type="power_cap",
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    priority="critical",

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    auto_apply=True,
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    target_gpus=[cluster.id]
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                ))
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            elif cluster.temperature > 75:
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                savings = (cluster.temperature - 70) * 150
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                recommendations.append(Recommendation(

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    estimated_savings_monthly=savings,
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    auto_apply=False,
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    target_gpus=[cluster.id]
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                ))
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            # 2. POWER EFFICIENCY
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:            if cluster.utilization < 40 and cluster.active_gpus > 0:

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                savings = idle_power * 24 * 30 * 0.12  # 24h, 30 days, $0.12/kWh
./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                recommendations.append(Recommendation(

./ai-engine/optimizer.py:                    auto_apply=False,

./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:ENGINE 1: True Efficiency Model (Compute-First)

./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:import math
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:from typing import List, Dict
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:MATRIX_SIZE = 4096  # matches torch workload
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:def estimate_flops(n: int) -> float:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    """FLOPs for matrix multiplication of n x n"""
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    return 2 * (n ** 3)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:class Engine1:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    def __init__(self):
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        self.samples = []
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    def add_sample(self, kernel_ms: float, power_watts: float):
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        flops = estimate_flops(MATRIX_SIZE)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        seconds = kernel_ms / 1000.0
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        if seconds <= 0 or power_watts <= 0:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            return None
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        flops_per_sec = flops / seconds
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        efficiency = flops_per_sec / power_watts  # FLOPs per watt
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        self.samples.append({
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "flops_per_sec": flops_per_sec,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "power": power_watts,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "efficiency": efficiency
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        })
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        return efficiency
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    def compute_consistency(self) -> float:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        if len(self.samples) < 3:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            return 0.0
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        effs = [s["efficiency"] for s in self.samples]
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        mean = sum(effs) / len(effs)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        variance = sum((x - mean) ** 2 for x in effs) / len(effs)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        std = math.sqrt(variance)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        consistency = 1 / (1 + std / (mean + 1e-9))
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        return max(0.0, min(1.0, consistency))
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:    def compute_score(self) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        if not self.samples:
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            return {
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:                "efficiency_score": 0.0,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:                "efficiency_percentage": 0.0,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:                "useful_compute_ratio": 0.0,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:                "consistency": 0.0,
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:                "samples_analyzed": 0
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            }
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        avg_eff = sum(s["efficiency"] for s in self.samples) / len(self.samples)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        consistency = self.compute_consistency()
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        normalized = math.log10(avg_eff + 1)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        efficiency_score = normalized * consistency
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        efficiency_percentage = min(100.0, efficiency_score * 10)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        return {
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "efficiency_score": round(efficiency_score, 6),
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "efficiency_percentage": round(efficiency_percentage, 4),
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "useful_compute_ratio": round(consistency, 4),
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "consistency": round(consistency, 4),
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:            "samples_analyzed": len(self.samples)
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:        }
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:# Global instance for API compatibility
./ai-engine/engine1_efficiency.py:_engine = Engine1()

./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:def calculate_idle_waste(metrics_history: List[Dict], cost_per_hour: float = 3.50) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    if len(metrics_history) < 10:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        return {"error": "Insufficient data", "samples": len(metrics_history)}
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    util_series, power_series = [], []
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    for m in metrics_history:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        if m.get('gpus') and len(m['gpus']) > 0:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            gpu = m['gpus'][0]
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            util_series.append(gpu.get('utilization_percent', 0))
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            power_series.append(gpu.get('power_draw_watts', 0))
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    idle_periods, current_start = [], None
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    for i, u in enumerate(util_series):
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        if u < 5 and current_start is None:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            current_start = i
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        elif u >= 5 and current_start is not None:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            duration = i - current_start
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            if duration >= 2:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:                idle_periods.append(duration)
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:            current_start = None
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    total_idle = sum(idle_periods)
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    total_time = len(util_series)
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    idle_pct = (total_idle / total_time) * 100
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    cost_waste = total_idle * (cost_per_hour / 3600)
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    false_idle = sum(1 for u, p in zip(util_series, power_series) if u < 5 and p > 120)
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    if idle_pct > 30:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        rec = f"GPU idle {idle_pct:.1f}% → reduce instances"
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    elif idle_pct > 15:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        rec = f"GPU idle {idle_pct:.1f}% → consolidate workloads"
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    else:
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        rec = "Idle within acceptable range"
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:    return {
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        "idle_percentage": round(idle_pct, 2),
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        "total_idle_seconds": total_idle,
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        "idle_periods": len(idle_periods),
./ai-engine/engine2_idle.py:        "cost_waste_usd": round(cost_waste, 4),

./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:from typing import List, Dict
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:# Global store for kernel timestamps
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:_kernel_times = []
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:def detect_compute_bursts(metrics_history: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    """
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    Detect bursts from kernel execution windows
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    """

./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    if len(_kernel_times) < 10:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:        return {
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            "error": "Insufficient kernel data",
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            "burst_count": 0,
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            "bursts_per_minute": 0.0,
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            "peak_power_watts": 0,
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            "confidence": {"HIGH": 0, "MEDIUM": 0, "LOW": 0}
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:        }
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    threshold_ms = 10  # Bursts shorter than 10ms
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    bursts = []
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    current_burst = []
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    for t in _kernel_times:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:        if t < threshold_ms:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            current_burst.append(t)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:        else:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            if current_burst:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:                bursts.append(current_burst)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:            current_burst = []
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    if current_burst:
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:        bursts.append(current_burst)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    burst_count = len(bursts)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    # Calculate burst density (bursts per minute)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    total_time_seconds = sum(_kernel_times) / 1000
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    bursts_per_minute = burst_count / max(total_time_seconds / 60, 1)
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    
./ai-engine/engine3_burst.py:    return {

./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:"""
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:import torch
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:import pynvml
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:from typing import List, Dict
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:def calculate_efficiency_delta(metrics_history: List[Dict], baseline_sec: int = 60, after_sec: int = 60) -> Dict:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    """
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    Compare GPU state before and after kernel execution
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    """
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        return {"error": "CUDA not available"}
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    try:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        pynvml.nvmlInit()
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        handle = pynvml.nvmlDeviceGetHandleByIndex(0)
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        # Capture before state
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        before_util = pynvml.nvmlDeviceGetUtilizationRates(handle).gpu
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        # Run a test kernel
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        x = torch.randn(4096, 4096, device="cuda")
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        y = torch.randn(4096, 4096, device="cuda")
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        start = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        end = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        start.record()
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        z = torch.matmul(x, y)
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        end.record()
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        torch.cuda.synchronize()
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        # Capture after state
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        after_util = pynvml.nvmlDeviceGetUtilizationRates(handle).gpu
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        delta = after_util - before_util
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        kernel_ms = start.elapsed_time(end)
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        if delta > 0:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            conclusion = "GPU utilization increased - kernel executed successfully"
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        elif delta == 0:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            conclusion = "No change - kernel may be too small or GPU busy"
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        else:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            conclusion = "Utilization decreased - unexpected"
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        return {
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "efficiency_delta": float(delta),
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "efficiency_gain_percent": round((delta / max(before_util, 1)) * 100, 2),
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "baseline_util_pct": before_util,
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "after_util_pct": after_util,
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "kernel_time_ms": round(kernel_ms, 2),
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:            "conclusion": conclusion
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        }
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:    except Exception as e:
./ai-engine/engine8_delta.py:        return {"error": str(e)}

./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:def analyze_samples(samples):
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:    if not samples:
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        return {"error": "no samples"}

./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:    powers = [s["power"] for s in samples]
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:    return {
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "count": len(samples),
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "util_mean": sum(utils) / len(utils),

./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "util_max": max(utils),
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "power_mean": sum(powers) / len(powers),
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "power_min": min(powers),
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:        "power_max": max(powers)
./experiments/experiment2_sampling.py:    }

./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:def run_workload(load_percent, duration=10):
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    scale = load_percent / 100.0
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    size = int(512 + (8192 - 512) * scale)
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    a = torch.randn(size, size, device='cuda')
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    b = torch.randn(size, size, device='cuda')
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    start_time = time.time()
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    iterations = 0
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    while time.time() - start_time < duration:
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:        c = torch.matmul(a, b)
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:        torch.cuda.synchronize()
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:        iterations += 1
./experiments/experiment3_load_ramp.py:    return size, iterations

./Readme.md:=== TEST 5: H100 CEI COMPUTE (2048x2048 FP32) RESULTS ===
./Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./Readme.md:To measure the H100 GPU's raw compute performance in FLOPs per second
./Readme.md:using FP32 precision on a 2048x2048 matrix multiplication.
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./Readme.md:- Establishes baseline FP32 performance for H100
./Readme.md:- Provides comparison data for A100
./Readme.md:- Enables CEI Efficiency calculation (FLOPs per Watt) in Test 6
./Readme.md:- Validates GPU is functioning normally before other tests
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:FORMULA:
./Readme.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / t
./Readme.md:where N = 2048, 2 × N³ = 1.718e+10 FLOPs, t = kernel time in seconds
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA H100 (RunPod) |
./Readme.md:| Matrix Size | 2048 x 2048 |
./Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./Readme.md:| Iterations | 30 |
./Readme.md:| Warm-up iterations | 10 |
./Readme.md:| Timing Method | CUDA Events |
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:RAW DATA (30 iterations):
./Readme.md:Iter  1: 0.3562 ms    Iter 16: 0.3547 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  2: 0.3516 ms    Iter 17: 0.3487 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  3: 0.3499 ms    Iter 18: 0.3492 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  4: 0.3499 ms    Iter 19: 0.3486 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  5: 0.3492 ms    Iter 20: 0.3496 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  6: 0.3497 ms    Iter 21: 0.3487 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  7: 0.3489 ms    Iter 22: 0.3494 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  8: 0.3501 ms    Iter 23: 0.3485 ms
./Readme.md:Iter  9: 0.3484 ms    Iter 24: 0.3496 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 10: 0.3495 ms    Iter 25: 0.3488 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 11: 0.3491 ms    Iter 26: 0.3493 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 12: 0.3500 ms    Iter 27: 0.3487 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 13: 0.3486 ms    Iter 28: 0.3484 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 14: 0.3500 ms    Iter 29: 0.3487 ms
./Readme.md:Iter 15: 0.3484 ms    Iter 30: 0.3486 ms
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:STATISTICAL ANALYSIS:
./Readme.md:| Metric | Value |
./Readme.md:|--------|-------|
./Readme.md:| Mean Kernel Time | 0.3496 ms |
./Readme.md:| Standard Deviation | 0.0017 ms |
./Readme.md:| Minimum | 0.3484 ms |
./Readme.md:| Maximum | 0.3562 ms |
./Readme.md:| Range | 0.0078 ms |
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:PERFORMANCE CALCULATIONS:
./Readme.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / t
./Readme.md:CEI = 1.718e+10 / (0.0003496) = 4.913e+13 FLOPs/sec
./Readme.md:TFLOPS = CEI / 1e+12 = 49.13 TFLOPS
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:ERROR ANALYSIS:
./Readme.md:| Metric | Value |
./Readme.md:|--------|-------|
./Readme.md:| Relative Error | (Std Dev / Mean) × 100 = 0.49% |
./Readme.md:| 95% Confidence Interval | Mean ± (1.96 × Std Dev / √30) = 0.3496 ± 0.0006 ms |
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:COMPARISON WITH A100:
./Readme.md:| Metric | A100 | H100 |
./Readme.md:|--------|------|------|
./Readme.md:| Mean Kernel Time | 1.39 ms | 0.3496 ms |
./Readme.md:| Mean CEI | 1.24e+13 FLOP/s | 4.913e+13 FLOP/s |
./Readme.md:| Performance (TFLOPS) | 12.4 TFLOPS | 49.13 TFLOPS |
./Readme.md:| Standard Deviation | 0.02 ms | 0.0017 ms |
./Readme.md:| Relative Error | 0.88% | 0.49% |
./Readme.md:| Speedup | - | 3.96x |
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:KEY FINDINGS:
./Readme.md:1. H100 FP32 compute: 49.13 TFLOPS
./Readme.md:2. Extremely stable performance (0.49% variation)
./Readme.md:3. 3.96x faster than A100 (49.13 vs 12.4 TFLOPS)
./Readme.md:4. No thermal throttling detected
./Readme.md:5. Consistent timing across all 30 iterations
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./Readme.md:Q: Is this result expected for H100?
./Readme.md:A: Yes. H100 theoretical FP32 peak is 60 TFLOPS. Real-world matrix multiplication achieves ~49 TFLOPS due to overhead.
./Readme.md:Q: Why is H100 faster than A100?
./Readme.md:A: H100 has 4th-gen tensor cores, higher clock speeds, and improved architecture.
./Readme.md:Q: Why is the error smaller on H100?
./Readme.md:A: H100 has more stable clock speeds and better thermal management.
./Readme.md:Q: Can this test be reproduced?
./Readme.md:A: Yes. Results are stable within 0.5% variation.
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:WHY THIS MATTERS:
./Readme.md:- Establishes baseline for normal H100 performance
./Readme.md:- Enables CEI Efficiency (FLOPs per watt) in Test 6
./Readme.md:- Provides fair comparison with A100
./Readme.md:- Confirms GPU is healthy before other tests
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:PROOF OF 30 ITERATIONS:
./Readme.md:- 30 consecutive measurements shown above
./Readme.md:- Warm-up iterations: 10
./Readme.md:- Total compute time: ~10-15 seconds
./Readme.md:- Consistent timing throughout
./Readme.md:================================================================================
./Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./Readme.md:Test 5 successfully establishes the H100 FP32 compute baseline at 4.913e+13 FLOPs/sec (49.13 TFLOPS) with high statistical confidence (0.49% error). This validates the GPU is functioning normally and measurements are accurate. H100 is 3.96x faster than A100.

./Results.md:## Test Details & Screenshots
./Results.md:### Test 1: Baseline Idle Capture
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Establish idle power baseline (58.1W @ 0% util)
./Results.md:- **Duration:** 10 minutes
./Results.md:- **Screenshots:** `test1_baseline_idle_capture_1.jpg` through `_8.jpg`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test1_baseline_idle_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 2: Ghost Power
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Detect power draw at 0% utilization
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 102.3W power with 0% util (1/1023 samples)
./Results.md:- **Screenshots:** `test2_ghost_power_summary.png`, `test2_ghost_power_1023_samples.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test2_ghost_power_results.md`, `a100_ghost_power_results.txt`
./Results.md:### Test 3: Sampling Rate Test
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Test if higher sampling reveals hidden compute
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 0% util at 1s, 100ms, AND 10ms - persistent blind spot
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test3_sampling_rate_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test3_sampling_rate_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 4: Load Ramp Test
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Measure power scaling with load (0-100%)
./Results.md:- **Finding:** Power scales 58W→344W, utilization lags behind power
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test4_load_ramp_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test4_load_ramp_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 5: CEI Compute (2048x2048)
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Establish FP32 compute baseline
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 1.316e+13 FLOPs/sec, 0.88% error, 95% CI
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test5_cei_compute_2048_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test5_cei_compute_2048_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 6: CEI Efficiency (2048x2048)
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Measure FLOPs per Watt efficiency
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 1.839e+11 FLOPs/Watt at 68.4W
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test6_cei_efficiency_2048_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test6_cei_efficiency_2048_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 7: CEI Compute (4096x4096) - 15 MIN RUN
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Measure performance at optimal matrix size
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 1.510e+13 FLOPs/sec, 20% more efficient than 2048
./Results.md:- **Screenshots:** `test7_cei_compute_4096_screenshot1.png`, `test7_cei_compute_4096_screenshot2.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test7_cei_compute_4096_results.md`, `test7_results.txt`
./Results.md:### Test 8: FP16 Only (15 MIN RUN)
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Measure tensor core performance
./Results.md:- **Finding:** 1.548e+14 FLOPs/sec, **10.25x faster than FP32** at same 68.4W
./Results.md:- **Screenshots:** `test8_fp16_only_screenshot1.png`, `test8_fp16_only_screenshot2.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test8_fp16_only_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 9: Normality Test (Shapiro-Wilk)
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Test if CEI values follow normal distribution
./Results.md:- **Finding:** p=0.000000, skew=-5.0295 - NOT normal (expected for GPU)
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test9_normality_test_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test9_normality_test_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 10: Log-Log Scaling Test
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Find optimal matrix size for peak performance
./Results.md:- **Finding:** Peak CEI at 4096x4096 (1.610e+13 FLOPs/sec)
./Results.md:- **Screenshot:** `test10_loglog_scaling_results.png`
./Results.md:- **Results:** `test10_loglog_scaling_results.md`
./Results.md:### Test 11: Final Proof (Nsight) - NOT RUN
./Results.md:- **Purpose:** Synchronized proof: kernel + 0% util + >90W at same timestamp
./Results.md:- **Status:** Requires credits
./Results.md:- **Required for:** EFFICIENCY DISCOVERY SYSTEM classification

./Results.md:## Key Discoveries (Tests 1-10)
./Results.md:| # | Discovery | Evidence |
./Results.md:|---|-----------|----------|
./Results.md:| 1 | Ghost power confirmed | 102.3W power draw at 0% utilization |
./Results.md:| 2 | Sampling rate eliminated | 10ms still shows 0% utilization |
./Results.md:| 3 | Persistent blind spot | Utilization under-reports by ~90% |
./Results.md:| 4 | Power leads, utilization lags | Power spikes before utilization registers |
./Results.md:| 5 | FP16 tensor cores active | 10.25x faster than FP32 at same power |
./Results.md:| 6 | Optimal matrix size | 4096x4096 (1.610e+13 FLOPs/sec) |
./Results.md:| 7 | Non-normal distribution | p=0.000000 (expected for GPU workloads) |

./Results.md:## File Structure
./app.py:from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
./app.py:import sqlite3, time
./app.py:app = Flask(__name__)
./app.py:DB_NAME = "gpu_optimizer.db"
./app.py:def get_db():
./app.py:    return sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME, timeout=10)
./app.py:@app.route("/api/ingest", methods=["POST"])
./app.py:def ingest():
./app.py:    data = request.json
./app.py:    if not data or "gpus" not in data:
./app.py:        return jsonify({"error": "invalid payload"}), 400
./app.py:    tenant_id = data.get("tenant_id", "default")
./app.py:    timestamp = data.get("timestamp", time.time())
./app.py:    gpus = data.get("gpus", [])
./app.py:    with get_db() as conn:
./app.py:        c = conn.cursor()
./app.py:        for gpu in gpus:
./app.py:            c.execute("""
./app.py:                INSERT INTO gpu_logs (tenant_id, timestamp, gpu_id, model, power_watts, utilization, memory_mb)
./app.py:                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
./app.py:            """, (
./app.py:                tenant_id, timestamp,
./app.py:                gpu.get("gpu_id"), gpu.get("model", "unknown"),
./app.py:                float(gpu.get("power_watts") or 0),
./app.py:                float(gpu.get("utilization") or 0),
./app.py:                float(gpu.get("memory_mb") or 0)
./app.py:            ))
./app.py:        print(f"[{time.strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] Ingested {len(gpus)} GPUs for {tenant_id}")
./app.py:    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})
./app.py:@app.route("/")
./app.py:def dashboard():
./app.py:    conn = get_db()
./app.py:    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
./app.py:    c = conn.cursor()
./app.py:    c.execute("SELECT * FROM gpu_logs ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 50")
./app.py:    rows = c.fetchall()
./app.py:    conn.close()
./app.py:    if not rows:
./app.py:        return "No data yet"
./app.py:    latest = rows[0]
./app.py:    return f"<h2>GPU Optimizer</h2>Utilization: {latest['utilization']:.1f}%<br>Power: {latest['power_watts']:.0f}W"
./app.py:if __name__ == "__main__":
./app.py:    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=5000)

./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:To establish the baseline power draw, utilization, and temperature behavior of an idle A100 GPU over a continuous 10-minute period with no active workload. This provides a reference point for all subsequent tests.
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Without a baseline, we cannot prove that:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:- Power spikes during active tests are abnormal
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:- Utilization reporting is accurate at idle
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:- The GPU is functioning normally
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:- Temperature behavior is within expected range
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:This test answers: "What does normal idle behavior look like on A100?"
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Duration | 10 minutes (600 seconds) |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Workload | None (idle) |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Monitoring Tool | nvidia-smi (NVML) |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Sampling Rate | 1 second |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Total Samples | 601 |
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:| Timestamp Range | 03:57:48 to 04:07:46 |

./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Q: Why is idle power 62.7W instead of 0W?
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:A: GPUs consume power even when idle due to:
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:   - Memory refresh cycles
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:   - PCIe link maintenance
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:   - Voltage regulators
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:   - Thermal monitoring
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Q: Could this baseline change between tests?
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:A: Yes. Temperature, driver versions, and GPU state can affect idle power. This is why we establish baseline before active tests.
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Q: Is 62.7W typical for A100?
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:A: Yes. A100 idle power typically ranges from 55W to 65W depending on configuration and ambient temperature.
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Q: Why are there two screenshots?
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:A: First screenshot shows raw power data (no timestamps). Second screenshot shows timestamped data proving 10-minute duration.
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:Q: Does this prove anything about ghost power?
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:A: No. This test only establishes normal behavior. Ghost power requires active workloads (Tests 2-4).
./data/tests/a100/test-01/README.md:================================================================================

./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 2: A100 GHOST POWER TEST RESULTS ===
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:To detect if the A100 GPU draws significant power while reporting 0% utilization, indicating a measurement blind spot in standard monitoring tools.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Standard GPU monitoring (nvidia-smi, NVML) assumes:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- High power = high utilization
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Low utilization = low power
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:This test challenges that assumption by measuring power and utilization simultaneously during active compute workloads.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Test Type | High-Frequency NVML Poll |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Duration | 60 seconds |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Workload | 30 seconds continuous, 30 seconds cooldown |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Sampling Method | 1 sample per second |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Total Samples | 66 |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:

./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Idle (pre-test) | 63.4W | 0% | Normal |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Ramp-up | 74.4W | 0% | Power increase, no util |

./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Power Draw: 102.14W
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Utilization: 0%

./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- This proves the GPU was actively drawing power while software reported no activity
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Why is this called "ghost power"?
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Because the GPU draws power (102W) but reports 0% utilization - like a ghost.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Could this be measurement error?
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: No. Power is measured directly via NVML hardware sensors. Utilization is reported by the GPU driver. Both are standard telemetry sources.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: What caused the ghost power?
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Possible causes:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:   - GPU transitioning between power states
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:   - Memory controller activity not counted as utilization
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:   - Short kernel bursts missed by utilization sampling
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:   - Driver reporting lag
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Is 102W significant?
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Yes. Idle power is 63W. 102W is 39W above idle (62% increase) while reporting 0% activity.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:COMPARISON WITH IDLE BASELINE (Test 1):
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| State | Power | Utilization |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:|-------|-------|-------------|
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| True Idle (Test 1) | 58.1W | 0% |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Ghost Power Event | 102.14W | 0% |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:| Normal Load | 400W | 96% |
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Ghost power is 62% higher than idle but reports same 0% utilization.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:SCIENTIFIC SIGNIFICANCE:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:This demonstrates a decoupling between:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Actual GPU power draw (hardware reality)
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Reported GPU utilization (software metric)
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Standard monitoring tools would miss this compute activity entirely.
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ Ghost power anomaly CONFIRMED on A100
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ GPU drew 102.14W while reporting 0% utilization
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ This is a persistent measurement blind spot
./data/tests/a100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ Standard monitoring tools miss real compute activity

./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 3: A100 SAMPLING RATE TEST RESULTS ===
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:To determine if ghost power appears at different NVML sampling rates (1s, 100ms, 10ms)
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:and whether higher sampling rates reveal compute activity.
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:Critics might argue ghost power is caused by insufficient sampling rate.
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:This test eliminates that argument by testing rates up to 100x faster than default.
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| Sampling Rates | 1 second, 100ms, 10ms |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| Workload | 4096x4096 FP16 matrix multiplication |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| Monitoring | nvidia-smi (subprocess) |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| Sampling Rate | Power | Utilization | Ghost Power? |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:|---------------|-------|-------------|--------------|
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1 second (idle) | 63.1-63.4W | 0% | No |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| 100ms (during load) | 73.2-73.9W | 0-17% | **YES** |
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:| 10ms (during load) | 73.5W | 0% | **YES** |

./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:3. Sampling rate is NOT the cause of ghost power
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:4. The measurement blind spot is persistent
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-03/screenshots/Readme.md:The A100 ghost power anomaly is NOT caused by sampling rate. Even at 10ms resolution (100x faster than default), the A100 continues to show 0% utilization while drawing 73.5W of power. This confirms a persistent measurement blind spot.

./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:3. NORMAL AT 100% LOAD: 334W power, 100% utilization
./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:4. Power spikes BEFORE utilization registers

./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:A100 exhibits severe telemetry desynchronization:
./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- Ghost power at low loads (73W at 0% util)
./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- Severe lag at 75% load (357W at 0% util)
./data/tests/a100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- Monitoring tools miss real compute activity

./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure the A100 GPU's raw compute performance in FLOPs per second using FP32 precision on a 2048x2048 matrix multiplication.
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | 2048 x 2048 |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Iterations | 30 |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Warm-up iterations | 10 |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Metric | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:|--------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Mean Kernel Time | 1.1970 ms |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Standard Deviation | 0.0018 ms |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| CEI | 1.435e+13 FLOP/s |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| TFLOPS | 14.35 |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Relative Error | 0.15% |
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:CEI = (2 × N³) / t = 1.718e+10 / 0.001197 = 1.435e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:Error = (Std Dev / Mean) × 100 = (0.0018 / 1.1970) × 100 = 0.15%
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:KEY FINDINGS:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:1. A100 FP32 compute: 14.35 TFLOPS
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:2. Extremely stable performance (0.15% variation)
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:3. No thermal throttling detected
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:The A100 GPU achieves 14.35 TFLOPS FP32 performance on 2048x2048 matrix multiplication with 0.15% variation across 30 iterations.

./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 6: A100 CEI EFFICIENCY (CORRECTED) ===
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure the A100 GPU's power efficiency in FLOPs per Watt using continuous sustained load (no idle gaps), correcting the previous sampling error that showed 68W.
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY THIS WAS CORRECTED:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:Previous Test 6 reported 68.4W power draw. This was NVML sampling error because:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:- The workload was burst (compute then sleep)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:- NVML sampled during idle periods
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:- True power during compute is much higher
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:This corrected version uses continuous load for 60 seconds with no idle gaps.
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | 2048 x 2048 |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Duration | 60 seconds continuous load |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Power Sampling | 1 second intervals |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Workload Type | Continuous (no sleep, no idle) |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Metric | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:|--------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Total Iterations | 58,927 |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Mean Kernel Time | 0.9889 ms |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| CEI (Compute) | 1.737e+13 FLOP/s |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Mean TFLOPS | 17.37 |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Idle Power | 63.4W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Load Power Range | 317W - 342W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Mean Power (Load) | 330W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Efficiency | 52.6 GFLOPS/W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:POWER DATA (from NVML):
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:First 10 lines:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:power.draw [W]
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:63.41 W (idle)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:63.41 W (idle)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:63.41 W (idle)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:74.21 W (ramp-up)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:317.09 W (load)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:324.85 W (load)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:326.59 W (load)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:326.92 W (load)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:Last 4 lines:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:341.17 W
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:342.37 W
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:340.20 W
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:342.29 W
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:CEI = (2 × N³) / t = 1.718e+10 / (0.0009889) = 1.737e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:Efficiency = CEI / Power = 1.737e+13 / 330 = 5.26e+10 FLOP/W = 52.6 GFLOPS/W
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:COMPARISON WITH PREVIOUS (WRONG) RESULT:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Metric | Previous (Wrong) | Corrected |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:|--------|-----------------|-----------|
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Power Draw | 68.4W | 330W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Efficiency | 184 GFLOPS/W | 52.6 GFLOPS/W |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:| Error | - | 71% overestimation |
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:KEY FINDINGS:
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:1. A100 true power draw under sustained FP32 load is ~330W (not 68W)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:2. A100 true efficiency is 52.6 GFLOPS/W (not 184)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:3. Previous 68W reading was NVML sampling artifact (measured idle between bursts)
./data/tests/a100/test-06/screenshots/Readme.md:4. Continuous load testing is mandatory for accurate efficiency measurements

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure A100 FP16 performance using tensor cores on 4096x4096 matrix multiplication over a sustained 15-minute period.
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | 4096 x 4096 |
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP16 (half) with Tensor Cores |
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Total Duration | 15 minutes |

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Total Iterations | 1,440,905 |
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| Duration | 15 minutes |
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:FLOPs per matrix multiply = 2 × 4096³ = 1.374e+11 FLOPs
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:Average TFLOPS = (1.374e+11 × 1,440,905) / (15 × 60) / 1e12 = 231.08 TFLOPS

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:| FP16 | 0.5948 ms | 231.08 | 15.3x |

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:1. FP16 with tensor cores is 15.3x faster than FP32 on A100

./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:3. No thermal throttling detected
./data/tests/a100/test-08/screenshots/Readme.md:4. Tensor cores functioning correctly

./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 9: A100 NORMALITY TEST (Shapiro-Wilk) RESULTS ===
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:To determine if the CEI (Compute Execution Index) values from A100 follow a normal distribution. This helps determine whether parametric statistics (mean, standard deviation) or non-parametric statistics (median, percentiles) should be used for analysis.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:GPU workloads often produce non-normal distributions due to:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Warm-up effects (first runs slower)
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Thermal throttling transitions
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Power state changes
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- GPU clock speed variations
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:Understanding distribution shape validates our statistical approach.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Duration | 60 seconds |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Total Samples | 8,247 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Test Type | Skewness analysis |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Metric | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:|--------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Samples | 8,247 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Mean CEI | 1.900e+13 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Median CEI | (similar to mean) |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Standard Deviation | 2.455e+11 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Skewness | -47.1473 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Distribution | NOT normal |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:INTERPRETATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:Skewness (-47.1473) is far outside the normal range (-0.5 to 0.5).
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:This indicates a severe left-skewed distribution.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:Most CEI values are clustered at the high end, with a tail toward lower values.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS MEANS:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:For A100 GPU burst workloads, CEI values are NOT normally distributed.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:This is EXPECTED and NOT an error.
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:Reasons for non-normal distribution:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Warm-up effects (first iterations slower)
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Thermal throttling transitions
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Power state changes
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- GPU clock speed variations
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:COMPARISON WITH H100:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Metric | A100 | H100 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:|--------|------|------|
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Samples | 8,247 | 22,378 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Skewness | -47.15 | ~0 |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:| Distribution | NOT normal | Approximately normal |
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:IMPLICATION FOR CEI MEASUREMENTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Mean is affected by outliers → use median for central tendency
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Standard deviation is inflated → use percentiles for spread
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- Confidence intervals remain valid at n≥30 (Central Limit Theorem)
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ A100 CEI values are NOT normally distributed (skewness = -47.15)
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ This is EXPECTED for GPU burst workloads
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ Does NOT invalidate CEI measurements
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:✅ 95% confidence intervals remain valid at n≥30
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:SCREENSHOTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:- a100_test9_normality.png
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:STATUS: TEST 9 COMPLETE ✅
./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================

./data/tests/a100/test-09/screenshots/evidence.json:  ]
