./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 10: A100 LOG-LOG SCALING TEST ===
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure A100 FP32 compute performance across different matrix sizes (512 to 4096)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:and observe scaling behavior using log-log analysis.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log-log scaling reveals how efficiently the GPU utilizes larger matrix sizes.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:The slope indicates performance scaling relative to theoretical FLOPs increase.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:This helps identify optimal matrix size for A100 workloads.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:FORMULAS USED:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / time
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:where N = matrix size, 2 × N³ = FLOPs per matrix multiplication
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log(Size) = log10(N)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log(CEI) = log10(CEI)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Theoretical scaling: CEI ∝ N³ (if perfect efficiency)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA A100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix sizes | 512, 1024, 2048, 4096 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Warm-up iterations | 10 per size |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Timing Method | CUDA Events |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | Time (s) | CEI (FLOPs/sec) | Log(Size) | Log(CEI) |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-------------|----------|-----------------|-----------|----------|
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 512 | 0.000057 | 4.673e+12 | 2.709 | 12.670 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1024 | 0.000179 | 1.198e+13 | 3.010 | 13.079 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 2048 | 0.001208 | 1.423e+13 | 3.311 | 13.153 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 4096 | 0.007726 | 1.779e+13 | 3.612 | 13.250 |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 512:  2 × 512³ = 2.68e+08 FLOPs / 0.000057s = 4.673e+12 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 1024: 2 × 1024³ = 2.15e+09 FLOPs / 0.000179s = 1.198e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 2048: 2 × 2048³ = 1.72e+10 FLOPs / 0.001208s = 1.423e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 4096: 2 × 4096³ = 1.37e+11 FLOPs / 0.007726s = 1.779e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:SCALING ANALYSIS:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Size Transition | Theoretical Ratio | Actual CEI Ratio | Efficiency |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------------|-------------------|------------------|------------|
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 512 → 1024 | 8.0x | 2.56x | 32.0% |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1024 → 2048 | 8.0x | 1.19x | 14.9% |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 2048 → 4096 | 8.0x | 1.25x | 15.6% |
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:KEY FINDINGS:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:1. CEI increases with matrix size (4.67e+12 → 1.78e+13 FLOP/s)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:2. Largest gain: 512 → 1024 (2.56x increase)
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:3. Peak performance: 17.79 TFLOPS at 4096x4096
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:4. Performance plateaus beyond 1024 due to memory bandwidth limits
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:The A100 GPU achieves peak FP32 performance of 17.79 TFLOPS at 4096x4096 matrix size.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Performance scales well from 512 to 1024, with diminishing returns beyond.
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:SCREENSHOTS:
./data/tests/a100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- a100_test10_loglog_scaling.png

./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Why is H100 idle power higher than A100?
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:A: H100 has more transistors (80B vs 54B), higher base clocks, HBM3 memory, and PCIe 5.0.
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Could this baseline change between tests?
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Yes. Temperature, driver versions, and GPU state can affect idle power.
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Is 69.5W typical for H100?
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Yes. H100 idle power typically ranges from 65W to 75W depending on configuration.
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Does this prove anything about ghost power?
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:A: No. This test only establishes normal behavior. Ghost power requires active workloads (Tests 2-4).

./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:| Test 2 (Ghost Power) | Compare idle power vs ghost power events |
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:| Test 3 (Sampling Rate) | Verify power consistency at different rates |
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:| Test 4 (Load Ramp) | Power scaling from idle to full load |
./data/tests/h100/test-01/screenshots/Readme.md:| Tests 5-10 (CEI) | Power measured against idle baseline for efficiency |

./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:SCIENTIFIC SIGNIFICANCE:
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:The A100 ghost power anomaly (102.3W at 0% utilization) is NOT present on H100.
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:H100 telemetry shows:
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Minimal power variation at idle (±0.25W)
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Accurate 0% utilization reporting
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- No measurement blind spot
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:This confirms ghost power is A100-specific, likely caused by:
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- NVML sampling window mismatch
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Power/utilization telemetry desynchronization
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:- Tensor core burst invisibility
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Why does H100 have higher idle power (75.6W vs A100 58.1W)?
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: H100 has more transistors (80B vs 54B), higher base clocks, HBM3 memory, and PCIe 5.0.
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Could ghost power appear on H100 with different workloads?
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Test 4 (load ramp) and Test 11 (burst workloads) confirm no ghost power.
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Is H100 telemetry more accurate than A100?
./data/tests/h100/test-02/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Yes. H100 shows no ghost power and linear power/utilization correlation.

./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure how H100 power draw and utilization scale with increasing compute load,
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:and compare against A100 which showed severe lag (343W power at 75% load but only 2% utilization).
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:A100 Test 4 revealed a decoupling between power and utilization:
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- 75% load: 343.7W power but only 2% utilization
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- Power increased BEFORE utilization registered
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:- Lower loads (0-50%) showed ghost power (68-69W at 0% util)
./data/tests/h100/test-04/screenshots/Readme.md:This test checks if H100 has the same observability problems.

./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 5: H100 CEI COMPUTE (2048x2048 FP32) RESULTS ===
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure the H100 GPU's raw compute performance in FLOPs per second
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:using FP32 precision on a 2048x2048 matrix multiplication.
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:- Establishes baseline FP32 performance for H100
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:- Provides comparison data for A100
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:- Enables CEI Efficiency calculation (FLOPs per Watt) in Test 6
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:- Validates GPU is functioning normally before other tests
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:FORMULA:
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / t
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:where N = 2048, 2 × N³ = 1.718e+10 FLOPs, t = kernel time in seconds
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA H100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | 2048 x 2048 |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Iterations | 30 |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Warm-up iterations | 10 |
./data/tests/h100/test-05/screenshots/Readme.md:| Timing Method | CUDA Events |

./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:To measure H100 power efficiency in FLOPs per Watt by combining compute performance (CEI) with actual power draw during sustained load.
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Data centers pay for electricity (kW/h)
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Higher FLOPs/Watt = lower operating costs
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Compares efficiency across different GPUs (A100 vs H100)
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Establishes baseline for optimizer improvements
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:FORMULAS USED:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / t
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:where N = 2048, 2 × N³ = 1.718e+10 FLOPs, t = kernel time in seconds
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:CEI_efficiency = CEI / Power
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:where Power = average GPU power draw in Watts during sustained load
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Efficiency (GFLOPS/W) = CEI_efficiency / 1e+9
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| GPU | NVIDIA H100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Matrix Size | 2048 x 2048 |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Duration | 5 minutes (305 seconds) |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Power Sampling | 1 second intervals |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Workload Type | Continuous (no sleep, no idle) |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:PROOF OF DURATION:

./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Last line: 642.29W (under load)
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:- Duration: 5 minutes 5 seconds ✅
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:RAW POWER DATA:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:First 3 lines:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:75.65 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:75.62 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Last 3 lines:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:642.04 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:642.53 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:642.29 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Step 1: CEI from Test 5
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:CEI = 4.913e+13 FLOPs/sec (49.13 TFLOPS)
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Step 2: Mean Power (from continuous load)
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Mean Power = 642 W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Step 3: Calculate Efficiency
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:CEI_efficiency = CEI / Power = 4.913e+13 / 642 = 7.65e+10 FLOPs/Watt
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Step 4: Convert to GFLOPS/W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Efficiency (GFLOPS/W) = 7.65e+10 / 1e+9 = 76.5 GFLOPS/W
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:RESULTS:

./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Mean CEI (Compute) | 4.913e+13 FLOPs/sec |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Mean Power Draw | 642 W |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Mean CEI Efficiency | 7.65e+10 FLOPs/Watt |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:| Efficiency (GFLOPS/W) | 76.5 GFLOPS/W |
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:================================================================================

./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:A: Yes. 2x more efficient (76.5 vs 38.5 GFLOPS/W).
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:Q: How was A100 power corrected?
./data/tests/h100/test-06/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-06/README.md:A: Original A100 Test 6 used burst workload (68W reading). Corrected continuous load shows true 321W.

./data/tests/h100/test-07/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-07/README.md:- 10-minute run confirms no thermal throttling or performance degradation
./data/tests/h100/test-07/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-07/README.md:- Provides baseline for comparison with A100
./data/tests/h100/test-07/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-07/README.md:- Validates that the GPU maintains stable performance over time
./data/tests/h100/test-07/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-07/README.md:================================================================================

./data/tests/h100/test-07/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-07/README.md:- GPU clocks are fully stabilized

./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:To determine if H100 kernel timing values follow a normal distribution after 60 seconds of continuous sampling.
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:- Validates whether parametric statistics (mean, standard deviation) are appropriate
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:- Compares stability against A100 which showed extreme skew (-5.03)
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:- 60 seconds at 100ms sampling provides 600+ samples for statistical confidence
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:FORMULA:
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:By Central Limit Theorem (CLT): For large sample sizes (n > 30), 
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:the sampling distribution of the mean approaches normal distribution
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:regardless of the underlying population distribution.
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:Skewness = Σ (x_i - x̄)³ / (n × σ³)
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:where 0 = symmetric, positive = right skew, negative = left skew
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| GPU | NVIDIA H100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Duration | 60 seconds |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Total Samples | 22,378 |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Sampling Rate | ~373 samples per second |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Workload | Continuous matrix multiplication (4096x4096 FP32) |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:| Timing Method | CUDA Events |
./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:================================================================================

./data/tests/h100/test-09/screenshots/data/tests/h100/test-09/README.md:- Calculated total compute time: 22,378 × 2.664 ms = 59.6 seconds ≈ 60 seconds ✅

./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:=== TEST 10: H100 LOG-LOG SCALING TEST ===
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:=== Manmohan Bains | May 8, 2026 ===
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS TEST WAS FOR:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:To measure H100 FP32 compute performance across different matrix sizes (512 to 4096)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:and observe scaling behavior using log-log analysis.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:WHY WE DID THIS TEST:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log-log scaling reveals how efficiently the GPU utilizes larger matrix sizes.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:The slope indicates performance scaling relative to theoretical FLOPs increase.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:This helps identify optimal matrix size for H100 workloads.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:FORMULAS USED:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CEI (Compute) = (2 × N³) / time
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:where N = matrix size, 2 × N³ = FLOPs per matrix multiplication
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log(Size) = log10(N)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Log(CEI) = log10(CEI)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Theoretical scaling: CEI ∝ N³ (if perfect efficiency)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:TEST CONFIGURATION:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Parameter | Value |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------|-------|
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| GPU | NVIDIA H100 (RunPod) |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Precision | FP32 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix sizes | 512, 1024, 2048, 4096 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Warm-up iterations | 10 per size |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Timing Method | CUDA Events |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:RESULTS:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | Time (s) | CEI (FLOPs/sec) | Log(Size) | Log(CEI) |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-------------|----------|-----------------|-----------|----------|
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 512 | 0.000038 | 7.14e+12 | 2.709 | 12.854 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1024 | 0.000071 | 3.01e+13 | 3.010 | 13.478 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 2048 | 0.000353 | 4.86e+13 | 3.311 | 13.687 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 4096 | 0.002660 | 5.17e+13 | 3.612 | 13.713 |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CALCULATIONS:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 512:  2 × 512³ = 2.68e+08 FLOPs / 0.000038s = 7.14e+12 FLOP/s
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 1024: 2 × 1024³ = 2.15e+09 FLOPs / 0.000071s = 3.01e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 2048: 2 × 2048³ = 1.72e+10 FLOPs / 0.000353s = 4.86e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:For 4096: 2 × 4096³ = 1.37e+11 FLOPs / 0.002660s = 5.17e+13 FLOP/s
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:SCALING ANALYSIS:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Size Transition | Theoretical Ratio | Actual CEI Ratio | Efficiency |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-----------------|-------------------|------------------|------------|
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 512 → 1024 | 8.0x | 4.21x | 52.6% |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1024 → 2048 | 8.0x | 1.61x | 20.1% |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 2048 → 4096 | 8.0x | 1.06x | 13.3% |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:COMPARISON WITH A100 (Test 10):
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| Matrix Size | A100 CEI | H100 CEI | H100 Speedup |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:|-------------|----------|----------|--------------|
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 512 | 4.87e+12 | 7.14e+12 | 1.47x |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 1024 | 1.14e+13 | 3.01e+13 | 2.64x |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 2048 | 1.43e+13 | 4.86e+13 | 3.40x |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:| 4096 | 1.61e+13 | 5.17e+13 | 3.21x |
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:KEY FINDINGS:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:1. CEI increases with matrix size (7.14e+12 → 5.17e+13 FLOP/s)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:2. Largest gain: 512 → 1024 (4.21x increase)
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:3. Performance plateaus beyond 2048
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:4. H100 is 3.2x faster than A100 at 4096x4096
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:5. Log-Log slope shows diminishing returns at larger sizes
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Why does performance plateau at larger matrix sizes?
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:A: Memory bandwidth and cache limitations become bottlenecks beyond 2048.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Why is H100 so much faster than A100 at 2048?
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:A: H100 has higher clock speeds and better memory bandwidth (HBM3).
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: What is the optimal matrix size for H100?
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:A: 2048-4096 range gives best performance, with 4096 achieving peak 51.7 TFLOPS.
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:Q: Does this test ghost power?
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:A: No. Ghost power appears during burst/transition workloads (Tests 2-4).
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:WHAT THIS PROVES:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- ✅ H100 FP32 performance scales with matrix size
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- ✅ Peak performance: 51.7 TFLOPS at 4096x4096
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- ✅ H100 is 3.2x faster than A100 at 4096x4096
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- ✅ Larger matrices show diminishing returns due to memory bandwidth limits
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:- ✅ Log-Log scaling confirms good utilization at moderate sizes
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:================================================================================
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:CONCLUSION:
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:The H100 GPU achieves peak FP32 performance of 51.7 TFLOPS at 4096x4096 matrix size, 
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:which is 3.2x faster than A100. Performance scales well from 512 to 2048, 
./data/tests/h100/test-10/screenshots/Readme.md:with diminishing returns beyond 2048 due to memory bandwidth limitations.

./db_init.py:def init_db():
./db_init.py:    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)
./db_init.py:    c = conn.cursor()
./db_init.py:    c.execute("""
./db_init.py:        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS gpu_logs (
./db_init.py:            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
./db_init.py:            tenant_id TEXT, timestamp REAL, gpu_id TEXT, model TEXT,
./db_init.py:            power_watts REAL, utilization REAL, memory_mb REAL
./db_init.py:        )
./db_init.py:    """)
./db_init.py:    c.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_gpu_time ON gpu_logs(gpu_id, timestamp);")
./db_init.py:    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
./db_init.py:    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL")
./db_init.py:    conn.commit()
./db_init.py:    conn.close()

./gpu_collector.py:import subprocess, time, requests
./gpu_collector.py:ENDPOINT = "http://YOUR_SERVER:5000/api/ingest"
./gpu_collector.py:TENANT_ID = "runpod_user_1"
./gpu_collector.py:INTERVAL = 30
./gpu_collector.py:def get_gpu_stats():
./gpu_collector.py:    try:
./gpu_collector.py:        models = subprocess.check_output(["nvidia-smi", "--query-gpu=name", "--format=csv,noheader"]).decode("utf-8").strip().split("\n")
./gpu_collector.py:        result = subprocess.check_output(["nvidia-smi", "--query-gpu=utilization.gpu,power.draw,memory.used", "--format=csv,noheader,nounits"]).decode("utf-8")
./gpu_collector.py:        stats = []
./gpu_collector.py:        for i, line in enumerate(result.strip().split("\n")):
./gpu_collector.py:            parts = [p.strip() for p in line.split(",")]
./gpu_collector.py:            if len(parts) < 3:
./gpu_collector.py:                continue
./gpu_collector.py:            stats.append({
./gpu_collector.py:                "gpu_id": str(i),
./gpu_collector.py:                "model": models[i] if i < len(models) else "unknown",
./gpu_collector.py:                "utilization": float(parts[0]),
./gpu_collector.py:                "power_watts": float(parts[1]),
./gpu_collector.py:                "memory_mb": float(parts[2])
./gpu_collector.py:            })
./gpu_collector.py:        return stats
./gpu_collector.py:    except Exception as e:
./gpu_collector.py:        print("nvidia-smi failed:", e)
./gpu_collector.py:        return []
./gpu_collector.py:def send():
./gpu_collector.py:    try:
./gpu_collector.py:        payload = {"tenant_id": TENANT_ID, "timestamp": time.time(), "gpus": get_gpu_stats()}
./gpu_collector.py:        r = requests.post(ENDPOINT, json=payload, timeout=5)
./gpu_collector.py:        if r.status_code != 200:
./gpu_collector.py:            print("Bad response:", r.text)
./gpu_collector.py:    except Exception as e:
./gpu_collector.py:        print("Error sending data:", e)
./gpu_collector.py:while True:
./gpu_collector.py:    start = time.time()
./gpu_collector.py:    send()
./gpu_collector.py:    elapsed = time.time() - start
./gpu_collector.py:    time.sleep(max(0, INTERVAL - elapsed))

./report_generator.py:import sqlite3, time
./report_generator.py:from fpdf import FPDF
./report_generator.py:DB_NAME = "gpu_optimizer.db"
./report_generator.py:price_per_kwh = 0.12
./report_generator.py:def get_data():
./report_generator.py:    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_NAME)
./report_generator.py:    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
./report_generator.py:    c = conn.cursor()
./report_generator.py:    c.execute("SELECT * FROM gpu_logs ORDER BY gpu_id, timestamp")
./report_generator.py:    rows = c.fetchall()
./report_generator.py:    conn.close()
./report_generator.py:    return rows
./report_generator.py:def generate_report():
./report_generator.py:    rows = get_data()
./report_generator.py:    if not rows:
./report_generator.py:        print("No data")
./report_generator.py:        return
./report_generator.py:    # Idle baseline (10th percentile)
./report_generator.py:    powers = sorted([r["power_watts"] for r in rows])
./report_generator.py:    idle_baseline = powers[int(len(powers) * 0.1)] if powers else 70
./report_generator.py:    prev_time = {}
./report_generator.py:    total_cost = 0
./report_generator.py:    idle_waste = 0
./report_generator.py:    idle_count = 0
./report_generator.py:    total_time = 0
./report_generator.py:    for r in rows:
./report_generator.py:        gpu_id = r["gpu_id"]
./report_generator.py:        ts = r["timestamp"]
./report_generator.py:        power = r["power_watts"]
./report_generator.py:        util = r["utilization"]
./report_generator.py:        mem = r["memory_mb"]
./report_generator.py:        if gpu_id in prev_time:
./report_generator.py:            delta = ts - prev_time[gpu_id]
./report_generator.py:            if delta > 120:
./report_generator.py:                delta = 30
./report_generator.py:            effective_power = max(0, power - idle_baseline)
./report_generator.py:            cost = (effective_power * delta) / 3_600_000 * price_per_kwh
./report_generator.py:            total_cost += cost
./report_generator.py:            total_time += delta
./report_generator.py:            is_idle = (util < 5 and mem < 500)
./report_generator.py:            if is_idle:
./report_generator.py:                idle_waste += cost
./report_generator.py:                idle_count += 1
./report_generator.py:        prev_time[gpu_id] = ts
./report_generator.py:    total_minutes = total_time / 60
./report_generator.py:    idle_pct = (idle_count / len(rows) * 100) if rows else 0
./report_generator.py:    monthly_waste = idle_waste * (30 * 24 * 60 / total_minutes) if total_minutes > 0 else 0
./report_generator.py:    pdf = FPDF()
./report_generator.py:    pdf.add_page()
./report_generator.py:    pdf.set_font("Arial", size=12)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt="GPU Optimizer Report", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Observation window: {total_minutes:.1f} minutes", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Idle power baseline: {idle_baseline:.0f}W", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Total cost: ${total_cost:.2f}", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Idle waste: ${idle_waste:.2f}", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Idle percentage of time: {idle_pct:.1f}%", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.cell(200, 10, txt=f"Estimated monthly waste (projected): ${monthly_waste:.2f}", ln=True)
./report_generator.py:    pdf.output("report.pdf")
./report_generator.py:    print("Report saved as report.pdf")
./report_generator.py:if __name__ == "__main__":
./report_generator.py:    generate_report()
